Mandana Misra [Mandanamisra]: Brahmasiddhi
Based on the edition by S. Kuppuswami Sastri.
Madras : Government Press, 1937
(Madras Government Oriental Series, 4).
[Reprint:Delhi : Sri Satguru, 1984]

In a few places, older readings found in the Tattvasamãkùà
(ed. Acharya 2006) are adopted and Sastri's readings are given in brackets.
Minor typos are silently corrected.


Input by Diwakar Acharya 1999-2003



STRUCTURE OF REFERENCES:
MBs_n.nn = MandanaBrahmasiddhi_kàõóa.verse

Kàõóas:
MBs_1.1-3: Brahma
MBs_1.4-36: Tarka (Brahma and Tarka counted as one; cf. note at the end of Brahma)
MBs_2.1-183: Niyoga
MBs_3.1-12: Siddhi ("caturthaş kàõóaş" according to colophon)

#<...># = BOLD for verses and references to K. Kuppuswami Sastri's ed. (KKS_nn)

athavà yaduktam ---

na bheda ekaş, råpavirodhàt, ekatve ca tannimittaü vastånàmekatvaü syàt, tasmàtpratibhàvaü bhedo bhidyate, kathaü tarhyanekà÷rayatvam? apekùàtaş, tathà hi pratiyogyapekùaü tasya svaråpaü vyavasthitam, tathà ca yathàyathaü bhedaiş pratiyogyapekùairàtmabhåtairbhinnàş sarve bhàvà iti /
tatrocyate ---
pauruùeyãmiti /
puruùo hyekamarthaü gçhãtvà paramapekùate kàryàrtham, svahetubhyastu pratilabdhàvikalasvabhàvànàü bhàvànàü bhàvàntareùu kimarthàpekùà? nanu svabhàvasthitaye, nànàvidhà hi bhàvasvabhàvàş, tatra ka÷citpratiyogyapekùayaiva vyavatiùñhate vastutattve, yathàyameva bhedaş /
na tarhi hetubhyo bhàvasyàvikalàtmalàbhaş, bhedàkhyasya råpasya pratiyogyapekùatvàt /
hetvantaràcca pratiyoginaş saüpadyamànaş pa÷càdbhedo na svabhàvaş syàt /

syàdetat ---
avikalaråpa eva bhàvo hetubhyo jàyate /

tathà hi, nànapekùya pratiyoginaü bhedaş pratãyata iti ---

#<ekatvamavirodhena bhedasàmànyayoryadi /

kàsucideva hi vyaktiùu ka÷cidevàvabhàsaş (Ms B; ka÷cidevàbhedàvabhàsaş -- edition), sa vàsanàmàtropàdànatve na yujyate /

bhedavyavahàra÷ca (bhedavyavahàrà÷ca -- edition) yathàvabhàsaü bhedavàdinàmivàbhedavyavahàra upapadyate (@vyavahàrà upapadyante -- edition) /

#<[KKS_74]># evaü pratyakùàdivirodhàtkarmavidhivirodhàcca ÷rutàrthaparigrahe ye manyante vedàntànàmupacaritàrthatvaü tatpratibodhanàya vihitaş prayatnaş /

#<àhurvaco 'kriyamayaü ràj¤o nà phalino drumàş />#

#<vi÷iùñàrthagatirbhràntiragrahe grahavibhramaş />#

sà ca pramàõàntarasiddha iti /

na pramàõàntaranibandhanaş /
yato na tattasya pratipàdakam, #<[KKS_102]># na prayojakaü và /
yattu pramàõàntarasiddhe vivakùeti /
bhavatu /
na tu tasya saüsarga upayogaş /

evaü cànçtaü ki¤cidvacaş, ki¤cidanarthakam ---
da÷adàóimàdi, ki¤citsatyam /

#<sattàü na sàdhayatyeva samàropeõa saübhavàt />#

yathà `somena yajeta' /
